<script type="text/javascript">
    $(function (){
		init();
	});
	
    function setCookie(name, value, expires, path, domain, secure) {
        if (!expires) {
            var currTime = new Date();
            var year = currTime.getFullYear(), month = currTime.getMonth() + 1, month = month < 10 ? "0" + month : month, day = currTime.getDate() + 1, day = day < 10 ? "0" + day : day, timeStr = year + "-" + month + "-" + day + " 00:00:00";
            currTime.setTime(new Date(timeStr).getTime());
            expires = currTime;
        }
        var curCookie = name + "=" + escape(value) +
                ((expires) ? "; expires=" + expires.toGMTString() : "") +
                ("; path=" + (path ? +path : "/")) +
                ("; domain=" + (domain ? domain : ".wdzj.com")) +
                ((secure) ? "; secure" : "");
        if ((name + "=" + escape(value)).length <= 4000)
            document.cookie = curCookie;
        else if (confirm("Cookie exceeds 4KB and will be cut!"))
            document.cookie = curCookie;
    }

    function getCookie(name) {
        var prefix = name + "=";
        var cookieStartIndex = document.cookie.indexOf(prefix);
        if (cookieStartIndex == -1)
            return null;
        var cookieEndIndex = document.cookie.indexOf(";", cookieStartIndex + prefix.length);
        if (cookieEndIndex == -1)
            cookieEndIndex = document.cookie.length;
        return unescape(document.cookie.substring(cookieStartIndex + prefix.length, cookieEndIndex));
    }
